        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For the chapter of the same name, see <a href="/wiki/Chapter_833" title="Chapter 833">Chapter 833</a>.</i></span></dd>
<dd><span class="dablink"><i>"Judge" redirects here.&#32;For the Legend of the Rainbow Island character, see <a href="/wiki/Judge_(Non-Canon)" title="Judge (Non-Canon)">Judge (Non-Canon)</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Vinsmoke Judge</b>, also known as <b>Garuda</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-Epithet_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Epithet-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> is the <a href="/wiki/King_(Title)" title="King (Title)">king</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Germa_Kingdom" title="Germa Kingdom">Germa Kingdom</a>, the supreme commander of the <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Royal" title="Royal">patriarch</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke Family</a>, being <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s biological father.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Judge is also a skilled <a href="/wiki/Scientist" title="Scientist">scientist</a> specialized in engineering and genetics, being responsible for the creation of most of Germa 66' technological advancements, including <a href="/wiki/Modified_Humans" title="Modified Humans">modifying</a> his own children into super soldiers and developing the <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">Raid Suit</a> that supports their enhanced abilities. He is a former member of <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>, where he was a research partner to the leading <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> scientist <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a> and helped in co-discovering the existence of the <a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a>, which years later, led to him building and expanding his Kingdom's military might through the use of <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">Cloning</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Scientist_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scientist-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> After escaping <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>, Judge and <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>, his former colleague, created <a href="/wiki/NEO_MADS" title="NEO MADS">NEO MADS</a> as a successor to MADS.<sup id="cite_ref-NEO_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NEO-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his actions, he is the secondary antagonist during the first half of the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island_Arc" title="Whole Cake Island Arc">Whole Cake Island Arc</a>. However, he and his children became allies of the Straw Hat Pirates and the Fire Tank Pirates after realizing Big Mom deceived and intended to assassinate them.<sup id="cite_ref-c870_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c870-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He is also one of the central characters in <a href="/wiki/Germa_66%27s_Ahh..._An_Emotionless_Excursion" title="Germa 66&#39;s Ahh... An Emotionless Excursion">Germa 66's Ahh... An Emotionless Excursion</a> Cover Page Serial.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Judge is a large man with long golden hair which reaches his waist. He has a long and thin black mustache which spikes upwards, a thin and small beard, and a prominent cleft chin. He always wears a golden helmet, which was later destroyed during his clash with Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Much like his children, Judge has curved eyebrows, although they are relatively thicker.
</p><p>He usually wears his <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">Raid Suit</a>, which is composed of a gray robe with the number "66" on the bottom front, a large orange cape, a belt with the number "66" on the buckle, dark gloves, and boots with jet propellers that allow him to levitate in the air once activated.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the <a href="/wiki/Tea_Party" title="Tea Party">Tea Party</a>, Judge changed into a dark grey suit, comprised of a grey shirt, white tie, trousers, and a double-breasted jacket. On top of the suit, he wore an orange, single-shoulder royal cloak clasped in front of his neck.<sup id="cite_ref-c860_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c860-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Thirteen years ago, Judge wore an outfit similar to the one he wears in the present, but with different coloring.<sup id="cite_ref-Past_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Past-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Judge did not wear a helmet during his time with MADS (thus exposing his eyebrows) and wore a simple suit instead of his Raid one. He was also far leaner and with shorter hair. His mustache would start growing around this time.
</p>

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Vinsmoke_Judge_at_Age_43.png/revision/latest?cb=20170903023410" class="image"><img alt="Vinsmoke Judge at Age 43" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="118" height="140" data-image-name="Vinsmoke Judge at Age 43.png" data-image-key="Vinsmoke_Judge_at_Age_43.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Vinsmoke_Judge_at_Age_43.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/118?cb=20170903023410" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Judge's appearance in Sanji's flashbacks.

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Judge_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest?cb=20181016034655" class="image"><img alt="Judge Anime Concept Art" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="96" height="140" data-image-name="Judge Anime Concept Art.png" data-image-key="Judge_Anime_Concept_Art.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Judge_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/96?cb=20181016034655" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Judge concept art from the anime.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/25/Log_Whole_Cake_Island_Alt.png/revision/latest?cb=20200704114948" class="image"><img alt="Log Whole Cake Island Alt" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="140" data-image-name="Log Whole Cake Island Alt.png" data-image-key="Log_Whole_Cake_Island_Alt.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/25/Log_Whole_Cake_Island_Alt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20200704114948" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Judge's attire from <a href="/wiki/Home_Video_Releases/Seasons_16-20" title="Home Video Releases/Seasons 16-20">One Piece Log Collection</a>.
</div></span></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Judge_Thousand_Storm.png/revision/latest?cb=20181027205146" class="image"><img alt="Judge Thousand Storm" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="73" height="140" data-image-name="Judge Thousand Storm.png" data-image-key="Judge_Thousand_Storm.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Judge_Thousand_Storm.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/73?cb=20181027205146" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Judge in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Thousand_Storm" title="One Piece Thousand Storm">One Piece Thousand Storm</a></i>.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Judge_Pirate_Warriors_4.png/revision/latest?cb=20200622025716" class="image"><img alt="Judge Pirate Warriors 4" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="140" height="129" data-image-name="Judge Pirate Warriors 4.png" data-image-key="Judge_Pirate_Warriors_4.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Judge_Pirate_Warriors_4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/140?cb=20200622025716" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Judge in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_4" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 4">One Piece: Pirate Warriors 4</a></i>.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3f/Vinsmoke_Judge_Bounty_Rush.png/revision/latest?cb=20230204040140" class="image"><img alt="Vinsmoke Judge Bounty Rush" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="106" height="140" data-image-name="Vinsmoke Judge Bounty Rush.png" data-image-key="Vinsmoke_Judge_Bounty_Rush.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3f/Vinsmoke_Judge_Bounty_Rush.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/106?cb=20230204040140" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Judge in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Bounty_Rush" title="One Piece Bounty Rush">One Piece Bounty Rush</a></i>.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Judge exhibits a typical royal hauteur, holding the firm belief that royalty is meant to be served, not to serve others. He disowned his third son, <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>, after learning about Sanji's "disgusting" habit of cooking for others (which he equates with serving others).<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> It has been shown that he passed these attitudes down to his children, as his other sons use the same rationale to justify bullying Sanji during their childhood.<sup id="cite_ref-Flashback_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Flashback-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> As part of this pride, Judge is preoccupied with recapturing the past glories of the Vinsmoke Family; for this reason, his lifelong ambition is to retake the entire <a href="/wiki/North_Blue" title="North Blue">North Blue</a>, as his ancestors once did.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> It was his desire for power and tremendous arrogance that nearly led to the deaths of himself and his family when Big Mom deceived him in forming an alliance only to betray and nearly kill him.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He has proven that he will not hesitate to use any means to accomplish his goals, including genetically modifying his children into <a href="/wiki/Modified_Humans" title="Modified Humans">superhumans</a>, and going as far as to tell his <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Sora" title="Vinsmoke Sora">wife</a> that he was content with turning their sons into monsters, as long as they win wars. When his wife maintained her opposition, he forced her to undergo the surgery which would install the modifications, and he was furious at his third son when he failed to exhibit any enhancements from the surgery.<sup id="cite_ref-Sora_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sora-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> As Sanji prepared to leave the family, Judge gave him the condition to never associate himself with Judge or the Vinsmoke name again, since he considers Sanji his greatest failure and shame.<sup id="cite_ref-c841_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c841-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Judge also loathes compassion and kindness, as he believes it makes people weak and useless; presumably for similar reasons, Judge does not seem too fond of chivalry (as seen when he called Sanji's chivalry a "bad influence" from Zeff). As such, he modified his sons to remove their emotions and ensure they would become strong while believing they were perfect. He expressed rage and despised Sanji heavily for showing such emotions, believing that Sora's kindness in helping the weak is worthless and greatly scorned Sanji due to his kindness. However, Judge was in disbelief when he saw Ichiji, Niji, and Yonji expressing a lack of care at their imminent demise after they fell into the Big Mom Pirates' trap. Even after witnessing the flaw in their design and seeing that the very emotions that Sanji possesses had saved him and his family, Judge still considers such emotions useless and cruelly mocked Sanji in front of Sanji's comrades. When he aided the Straw Hats against <a href="/wiki/Smoothie" class="mw-redirect" title="Smoothie">Smoothie</a>'s fleet, he angrily yelled at Luffy, demanding to know why he had traveled to <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a> to save Sanji while listing off all the things he despises about Sanji (e.g compassion and having emotions). When Luffy simply thanked Judge for aiding them, Judge was furious and continuously questioned the Straw Hat captain as the Straw Hats sailed away.
</p><p>As a king, Judge has exhibited significant political astuteness. He understood the full implications of <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Doflamingo</a>'s fall from power, including its impact on the war on <a href="/wiki/Broc_Coli_Island" title="Broc Coli Island">Broc Coli Island</a>. He also weighed up Germa's current privileges within the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> against the benefits of an alliance with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, before deciding that losing the right to attend <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a> was far exceeded by gaining the manpower to retake North Blue.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He is naturally cautious when making major political moves, and is conscious not to make commitments without taking measures to avert potential difficulties; when dealing with Big Mom, he sought out his estranged third son specifically because any threat or danger to Sanji would not affect him, and he planned to hold Pudding hostage in the Germa Kingdom to prevent Big Mom from backstabbing him after the wedding.<sup id="cite_ref-c849_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c849-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> However, Judge still underestimated Big Mom's capacity for betrayal, as he was unaware of her plans to double-cross him before the wedding even concluded.<sup id="cite_ref-c850_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c850-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Even though he puts up a cautious defense when dealing with pirates, he nevertheless believed that even criminals such as them would have some honor in keeping with their deals, and became horrified when this view was betrayed.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Judge has also exhibited great respect for strength, and the privileges that come with its exercise. He believes that men should speak with physical force alone, and flaunts his own power and accomplishments by hanging an image of himself victorious in the <a href="/wiki/Conquest_of_Four_Nations" title="Conquest of Four Nations">Conquest of Four Nations</a> as interior decoration inside his castle.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> This view also colors his attitude towards his children, as he only values them when they prove such strength; for this reason, he refused to intervene as his other sons constantly and viciously bullied Sanji when they were all children.<sup id="cite_ref-Flashback_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Flashback-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> By contrast, he doted on all his other children, whose superhuman physical strength became obvious even as children. Even after 13 years of estrangement, after which Sanji returned to the Germa Kingdom with significantly improved physical strength that surprised even him, Judge still refused to acknowledge Sanji as his son.<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Judge is also extremely hypocritical. While he has emotions himself, he despises Sanji for his kindness and because he did not receive the same modifications as his brothers. While he refuses to privately acknowledge Sanji as a son, he openly acknowledges him in front of guests and allies in order to make himself look like a benevolent father and expresses rage that Sanji would dare to attack his father or sacrifice his family for his crew. When he was in a situation where his life was at stake, he was quick to act extremely cowardly, begging someone to save him while crying. Judge also believes that everyone should have some form of honor, but he has no qualms in using underhanded tactics such as blackmailing Sanji into an arranged marriage or lying to others to satisfy his own selfish agenda. While he claims he isn't inhuman enough to kill his own son, he has no problem in allowing others or Sanji himself to do it for him.
</p><p>In addition, Judge has proven that he is capable of immense cruelty. He was not simply content with demoralizing Sanji in front of his siblings, but further punished him by putting a metal mask over his face and locking him up in a dark cell within the family's castle. He also did nothing when Sanji's brothers were brutally bullying him and coldly told the latter he was not a son worth helping. After 13 years apart, his only reason for seeking Sanji out was to use him as a political pawn to further his goals and outright stated he views him as a means to an end. He even threatened the life of <a href="/wiki/Zeff" title="Zeff">Zeff</a><sup id="cite_ref-Zeff_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zeff-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> (the man who took Sanji in after Sanji left the family) and placed exploding wrist-cuffs on Sanji's hands (the things Sanji values the most), to ensure Sanji cooperated with the wedding.<sup id="cite_ref-Cuffs_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuffs-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> The only time he has shown an interest in Sanji's safety was in preventing Niji from attacking him, because he still needed Sanji to seal the political alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Despite his cruelty, however, Judge claims that he is not inhumane enough to kill his children, regardless of his feelings toward them. Despite considering Sanji as an utterly worthless son and a disgrace to the Vinsmoke Family, Judge chose to condemn his third son to life imprisonment instead of putting him to death. When Sanji decided to leave, Judge allowed Sanji to flee the Germa Kingdom, believing that Sanji would never survive on his own on the high seas.<sup id="cite_ref-c841_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c841-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Judge_Cries.png/revision/latest?cb=20180429034544" class="image"><img alt="Judge Cries" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Judge Cries.png" data-image-key="Judge_Cries.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Judge_Cries.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180429034544" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Judge_Cries.png/revision/latest?cb=20180429034544" class="image"><img alt="Judge Cries" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Judge_Cries.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180429034544" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Judge Cries.png" data-image-key="Judge_Cries.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Judge_Cries.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180429034544" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Judge_Cries.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Judge cries in despair.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Judge believes that the strong has the right to oppress the weak, he hypocritically shows great fear and despair when he is subjected to the short end of such treatment. When the Charlotte Family revealed Big Mom's plan to massacre his entire family and rendered them powerless with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Pero_Pero_no_Mi" title="Pero Pero no Mi">binding candy</a>, Judge became horrified and sank into despair, weeping in the face of imminent doom and lamenting that his lifelong ambition of taking back North Blue would be beyond his reach. While crying, Judge was mocked by Ichiji, his child that he ensured would be strong and have no emotion, while also seeing Niji and Yonji simply accepting death without any resistance and even laughing about it. Seeing this flaw in their engineered apathy, Judge accusingly stated something is wrong with them, being unable to see that it was his own selfish actions that removed their capacity to feel emotions.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Judge confronted Big Mom, he showed some honor as he acknowledged his dream of retaking the North Blue was overreaching as he cursed Big Mom for deceiving him.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> To repay his debt with Sanji, Judge chose to aid the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> at <a href="/wiki/Cacao_Island" title="Cacao Island">Cacao Island</a> rather than fleeing Totto Land.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sora">Sora</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Judge and his <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Sora" title="Vinsmoke Sora">wife</a> had conflicting ideals. Sora did not want their sons to lose their humanity, but Judge only cared about giving them the power to win wars and forced her to undergo surgery which would alter their sons' <a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a>. Sora did everything she could to stop Judge's wild ambitions, even if it meant risking her own life.<sup id="cite_ref-Sora_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sora-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After she passed away, Judge wished to move on from her way of doing things, as he saw no merit and nothing to be gained by continuing on the legacy of a deceased person.<sup id="cite_ref-Past_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Past-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He forbade Sanji from emulating her example, even scorning him for following her legacy of caring for the weak. Judge effectively trampled on Sora's wishes, genetically modifying their quadruplet sons against her will and later neglecting, imprisoning, and banishing Sanji, their only son to live up to Sora's efforts.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sanji">Sanji</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Sanji is Germa’s failure! His skin doesn’t work as a shield! He works as a cook because he has no pride in his royal blood! He’s easily moved like an idiot and his soft mind makes him puts his life on the line for the weak! A failed soldier who is far from perfect… That’s all he is!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Judge to Luffy about how pathetic Sanji is as Judge’s son.</cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>Unlike his siblings, whose genetic modifications were successful in giving them superhuman strength, <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s strength remained that of a normal human throughout his childhood, due to <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Sora" title="Vinsmoke Sora">Sora</a>'s intake of a counter-drug that negated the surgery effects on Sanji alone. Judge did try to encourage Sanji by sternly scolding him that he must train a thousand times harder than his siblings if he wished to become strong, but he still showed no improvement. After Sora's death, Judge blamed Sanji and saw him as a constant reminder of his late wife's personality. For this reason, Judge allowed his other sons to bully Sanji, even stating that he was not obligated to help the pleading Sanji and deeming him as a disgrace.
</p><p>Judge viewed Sanji to be an "utter waste of space and air" and the single blemish in his life. This even led the pitiless father to have Sanji locked in a dungeon for over six months. Despite his extreme scorn for Sanji, Judge allowed Sanji to be fed and admitted that he could never bring himself to dispose of Sanji himself. When Sanji escaped from his cell and announced his intentions to leave the Germa Kingdom, Judge was pleased and even allowed Sanji to go as he thought Sanji would die on his own. He allowed Sanji to leave on the condition that he never tell anyone about their relationship as he was the only thing, he was most ashamed of, which left his son in tears. <sup id="cite_ref-c841_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c841-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Judge, however, soon decided to bring him back and pursued him constantly, going so far as to both use the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> to locate him, and manipulating the Marines' <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty system</a> to ensure his safe return.<sup id="cite_ref-c826_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c826-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> This was all done merely in furtherance of his ambition to re-conquer the North Blue. In order to seal an alliance with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, which would give him the forces necessary to realize this ambition, he forced Sanji to marry <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">one of Big Mom's daughters</a> in order to meet her terms for an alliance. During their reunion, they expressed their mutual dislike for each another, with Sanji refusing to acknowledge him as his father,<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> and Judge telling Sanji that he never considered Sanji a true son, even after Sanji proved himself to have grown tremendously during his decade of absence.<sup id="cite_ref-Cuffs_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuffs-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Judge finds Sanji's unroyal behavior disgraceful, claiming Sanji needed to reign in his "twisted thinking". Because he viewed Sanji as a means to an end, he required him to be alive in order for his plan to be a success as shown when he prevented Niji from attacking him, which marked the first time he ever defended Sanji from his brothers. As Sanji reiterated his disgust for his family, Judge quelled Sanji's rebellious behavior by threatening the life of <a href="/wiki/Zeff" title="Zeff">the man</a> whom he saw as his real father.<sup id="cite_ref-Zeff_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zeff-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He is also observant of Sanji's behavior since their reunion, as he noticed his third son gone pale when he revealed his knowledge of Zeff's existence, and when Luffy came towards the Vinsmoke carriage, his only reaction was looking back at his son. On the night before the wedding, Judge and his sons then shared a toast to Sanji, albeit in a patronizing way, for actually being useful to them.<sup id="cite_ref-c856_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c856-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In keeping with his utmost respect for strength, Judge claimed that Sanji, even as a child, was worthless for not being able to defend himself from his brothers and punished him for persisting with cooking. However, he (like Reiju and Yonji) did show surprise at Sanji's drastically improved physical strength as an adult, voicing his disbelief that Sanji was able to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Haki</a> in their fight. He also expressed surprise and anger that Sanji would dare to kick him or that he'd sacrifice his own family just to protect his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite their mutual dislike, Sanji confessed to Luffy that he did not have in him to leave his father to die at Big Mom's hand and wanted to save him.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> This was later showed to be an ironic comparison between Sanji's brothers, who Judge had always favored, while looking down on Sanji for retaining his sense of compassion. It was Sanji's possession of emotions that drove him to save his father and siblings compared to how Sanji's brothers, because of their lack of emotions, simply accepted the incoming demise of both their father and their own while not bothering to show any resistance. After being held at gunpoint by the Big Mom Pirates, Judge was utterly shocked when Sanji freed him and his other children.<sup id="cite_ref-Freed_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Freed-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Sanji_Disowns_Judge.png/revision/latest?cb=20230218012329" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Disowns Judge" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sanji Disowns Judge.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Disowns_Judge.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Sanji_Disowns_Judge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230218012329" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Sanji_Disowns_Judge.png/revision/latest?cb=20230218012329" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Disowns Judge" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Sanji_Disowns_Judge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230218012329" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sanji Disowns Judge.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Disowns_Judge.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Sanji_Disowns_Judge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230218012329" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sanji_Disowns_Judge.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sanji disowns his father after rescuing him.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After being freed by Sanji, Judge begrudgingly listened to his son when the latter pointed him to retreat into Bege's giant castle.<sup id="cite_ref-c869_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c869-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> After entering Bege's castle, Judge overheard Nami saying that it was Sanji's wish to save them. He then questioned Sanji on why he saved them in spite of his hatred of them, even stating that it was the perfect opportunity to be rid of them. Sanji answered by saying he did not want to disappoint his <a href="/wiki/Zeff" title="Zeff">"father"</a> by stooping so low as to allow his biological family to die. Sanji then angrily grabbed Judge, stating that he is not his father anymore and demanded him to never show his face around him or his crew ever again. Recognizing the pain, he put Sanji through and the debt he owed him, Judge solemnly agreed to never interfere with Sanji's life ever again nor go near the East Blue again. He then offered to distract Big Mom to give the alliance an opening to escape as he did not want to be in debt to a "failure" as Sanji understood Judge's resolve. However, Sanji still aided his family in fighting off the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c870_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c870-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Judge and his forces once again came to Sanji's aid at <a href="/wiki/Cacao_Island" title="Cacao Island">Cacao Island</a>. Judge shared a glare with Sanji while asking Luffy why he risked his life for Sanji's sake. Judge also still referred to Sanji as Germa's failure and stated all his "faults" to the retrieval team.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Presently, Judge is completely unaware that the genetic modifications he gave Sanji have finally awakened. <sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Reiju">Reiju</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Vinsmoke_Judge%27s_Fatherly_Side.png/revision/latest?cb=20170903020309" class="image"><img alt="Vinsmoke Judge&#39;s Fatherly Side" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vinsmoke Judge&#39;s Fatherly Side.png" data-image-key="Vinsmoke_Judge%27s_Fatherly_Side.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Vinsmoke_Judge%27s_Fatherly_Side.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170903020309" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Vinsmoke_Judge%27s_Fatherly_Side.png/revision/latest?cb=20170903020309" class="image"><img alt="Vinsmoke Judge&#39;s Fatherly Side" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Vinsmoke_Judge%27s_Fatherly_Side.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170903020309" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vinsmoke Judge&#39;s Fatherly Side.png" data-image-key="Vinsmoke_Judge%27s_Fatherly_Side.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Vinsmoke_Judge%27s_Fatherly_Side.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170903020309" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vinsmoke_Judge%27s_Fatherly_Side.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Judge embraces four of his children.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Judge's <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Reiju" title="Vinsmoke Reiju">daughter</a> outwardly shows great respect and admiration for him; while Sanji denounces Judge's decision to put up glorified pictures of himself throughout the royal castle, Reiju responds that it simply shows that their father is a man of great fame and power.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Judge, in turn, trusts Reiju enough to delegate important tasks to her, such as cuffing Sanji with exploding wristlets.
</p><p>Unbeknownst to Judge, however, Reiju secretly holds him in contempt for contributing to her mother's death, and for his cruel ways (including his treatment of Sanji). Even though Judge has modified her so that she cannot directly disobey his orders, she still circumvents him when she can, such as deciding to put fake exploding bracelets onto Sanji when trusted with the task. Her hatred of her father's cruelty extends to the point that she wishes death on him as well as herself for the things he had forced her to do, reasoning that there's no place in the world for murderers.<sup id="cite_ref-Sora_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sora-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the Vinsmoke Family was facing imminent doom from Big Mom's treachery, Judge panicked while Ichiji, Niji, and Yonji were nonchalant as Reiju silently acknowledged that her father was the one at fault for removing their capacity to feel emotions.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite her resentment towards him, she expressed worry for her father when he charged at Big Mom and was easily taken down.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ichiji">Ichiji</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Judge highly values his "beloved" <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Ichiji" title="Vinsmoke Ichiji">eldest son</a>, and is happy to entrust the command of Germa 66 forces to him as the organization carries out its commissions. He approved of Ichiji (along with Niji and Yonji) bullying Sanji as a child,<sup id="cite_ref-Flashback_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Flashback-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> and refused to consider marrying him off to one of Big Mom's daughters even to seal a powerful political alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-Cuffs_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuffs-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Ichiji informed Sanji that he was disgracing the family with his unroyal behavior, Judge approved of his eldest son's words, stating Ichiji's logic was "flawless". 
</p><p>Ironically, when the Big Mom Pirates were holding the Vinsmokes at gunpoint, Ichiji and his two brothers remained calm while Judge panicked. Right after Ichiji called his father's pleas to Big Mom pathetic, Judge accusingly retorted that something is wrong with the three brothers. In his desperate panic, Judge was unable to see that he was responsible for removing Ichiji's capacity to feel emotion.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Niji">Niji</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As with Ichiji, Judge also values his <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Niji" title="Vinsmoke Niji">second son</a> and is happy to entrust Germa 66 forces to him in combat situations. He approved of Niji (along with Ichiji and Yonji) bullying Sanji as a child,<sup id="cite_ref-Flashback_13-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Flashback-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> and refused to consider marrying him off to one of Big Mom's daughters even to seal a powerful political alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-Cuffs_23-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuffs-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Though he has great respect for his second son, Judge still stopped Niji from kicking Sanji, not willing to let Sanji get damaged before the wedding. Niji is also obedient to his father, as he halted his attack on Sanji at his father's orders despite his extreme fury towards his younger brother. However, when Niji simply laughed off the situation where the Charlotte Family had them at gunpoint, Judge accusingly retorted that something is wrong with the three brothers. Ironically, Judge was responsible for Niji's incapacity to feel emotion.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In spite of this, Niji did show some concern for his father. He didn't hesitate to rush to his aid after he was struck down by Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_9-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> When the Chateau collapsed, Niji and Yonji quickly rescued their unconscious father and took him far from the destruction.<sup id="cite_ref-c872_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c872-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Yonji">Yonji</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Judge seems to respect his <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Yonji" title="Vinsmoke Yonji">youngest son</a>, questioning Sanji over what he did to his younger brother and stating that Yonji's strength is formidable.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> He considers Yonji, along with Ichiji and Niji, as "valuable"; therefore, despite his desire for an alliance with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, he refused to consider marrying Yonji into her family in order to meet her terms for an alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-Cuffs_23-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuffs-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> However, when Yonji looked apathetically at the situation where the Charlotte Family had them at gunpoint, Judge accusingly retorted that something is wrong with the three brothers. In this panicking moment, Judge was unable to see that he was responsible for Yonji's incapacity to feel emotion.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In spite of this, Yonji did show some concern for his father. He didn't hesitate to rush to his father's aid after he was struck down by Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_9-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> When the Chateau collapsed, Yonji and Niji quickly rescued their unconscious father and took him far from the destruction.<sup id="cite_ref-c872_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c872-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Germa_Kingdom">Germa Kingdom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As king of his country, Judge demands the utmost respect from his people. The citizens, which are mainly made up of his soldiers and maids, are fiercely loyal and obedient to him and all highly respect Judge as their king. They follow his rule and demand in waging wars or leading the Germa 66 obediently, as Judge considers his men the backbone of the Germa Kingdom. Judge highly values his science unit, as he uses them to ensure his army is strong and fruitful in his conquest.
</p><p>Despite their loyalty, Judge cares very little to none for his people, as he was more concerned in reconquering the North Blue over retaining his kingdom's connection to the World Government and the privileges that came with it. Indeed, as the Big Mom Pirates held him and his family at gunpoint, Judge only lamented that his lifelong dream of conquering the North Blue would never come true rather than care that his family and his entire kingdom would be destroyed by Big Mom just to get their technology. Because of Judge's actions, his entire kingdom has lost all political connections to the World Government.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Subordinates">Subordinates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Judge describes the <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">soldiers</a> of Germa 66 as the "true backbone of Germa's might", and he expects their absolute loyalty. However, Judge cares nothing for his soldiers, as he ordered several of them to block Sanji's attack, and even stabbed one of them through with a spear simply to land a surprise attack on Sanji without hesitation or remorse.<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> This also extends towards his servants, as when Niji attacked Cosette over a trivial matter, he did nothing nor showed any remorse after Niji brutally injured her. He firmly stated that his servants are meant to serve and not the other way around.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Allies">Allies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Judge originally was very apathetic towards the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, most likely due to his arrogant royal values, but was angered when Sanji claimed he would sacrifice his own family to be with his crew. Judge later recognized the infamous <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> as he rushed towards their carriage but was nonplussed when Luffy tried to get Sanji to return to the crew. During their encounter, Judge watched Sanji carefully and taking note of Sanji's reaction. When Sanji was forced to beat down his captain and <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> slapped Sanji in farewell, Judge believed with satisfaction that Sanji had severed his "useless bonds".<sup id="cite_ref-c844_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c844-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the wedding, he was surprised to see them causing chaos and deduced that they were there to rescue Sanji, leaving him both shocked and furious at the depths they would go to save him, and in the anime stated he would attack them for their actions.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> After the Big Mom Pirates revealed their treachery to the Vinsmokes and prepared to assassinate them, it was thanks to Luffy's efforts that Sanji was able to free Judge and his other children from their restraints. As Big Mom screamed, Chopper placed earplugs into his ears and Nami returned the Vinsmokes' <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">raid suit</a> to him and his children before they join forces with the Straw Hat Pirates and the Fire Tank Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-Freed_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Freed-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> When Judge assisted the Straw Hats in escaping <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Smoothie" title="Charlotte Smoothie">Smoothie</a>'s fleet, he asked Luffy why he risked his life just to save Sanji. Instead of answering him, Luffy simply thanked him for his help and fled with his crew, which infuriated Judge.<sup id="cite_ref-c899_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c899-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fire_Tank_Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the Vinsmoke Family were deceived by Big Mom, Judge and his children briefly allied with the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a>. To help Bege and his allies escape the wedding venue, Judge volunteered to confront the Big Mom Pirates in order to give them the opening they need.<sup id="cite_ref-c870_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c870-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Caesar_Clown">Caesar Clown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Judge was once a colleague with fellow <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a> scientist <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>, when both worked with Vegapunk conducting unlawful and sometimes unethical experiments behind the World Government. At present day, Caesar would not hesitate to calling out Judge for his overbearing attitude.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> The feeling appears to be mutual as the two had a prior fallout after Vegapunk was nominated as recipient for the Ibel Peace Prize over his fellow MADS colleagues; a fact Judge would never forget as he continued to pick a fight with Caesar after his escape to the <a href="/wiki/Germa_Kingdom" title="Germa Kingdom">Germa Kingdom</a>. They do have a mutual relationship when blaming the fault on Vegapunk. Upon coming to a consensus that Vegapunk was the obstacle that prevented them from the top spot, Judge and Caesar set aside their differences and together formed a successor of their old group known as <a href="/wiki/NEO_MADS" title="NEO MADS">NEO MADS</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1067_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1067-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Blue">North Blue</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Judge claims that the countries of <a href="/wiki/North_Blue" title="North Blue">North Blue</a> are his enemies. He has spent his entire life dedicated to taking revenge against those countries in order to restore his Germa Empire. The reason he allied with the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a> is to gain the military forces to achieve this goal,<sup id="cite_ref-Cuffs_23-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuffs-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> and when they betrayed him, he tearfully lamented that he would be unable to fulfill his ambition of taking back the quadrant of the sea his ancestors once held.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlotte_Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Our dreams are dust!! What am I to say to the ghosts that have not land to step foot on, after those short 66 days of hope? We entrusted you with our 300 year old desires, the chagrin of our people! Curse you, foul villain!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Judge cursing Big Mom for her betrayal.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_9-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
Judge desired an alliance with Big Mom, as her forces, combined with <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">his</a>, would enable him to easily conquer North Blue. However, he does not like her as a person, calling her a "madwoman" and not wanting his favored children to be married into her <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">family</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Cuffs_23-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuffs-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> In front of her, Judge would put up a front of friendly and respectful relationship, though full-heartedly agreeing with her on the marriage's primary reason is to cement the alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-c845_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c845-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Judge planned to take Pudding hostage after the wedding in order to ensure that Big Mom won't double-cross him.<sup id="cite_ref-c849_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c849-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
