</p><p>However, in truth, Big Mom also dislikes Judge and his children and refers to them as the "annoying leadership".<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> In fact, she never intended to form an alliance between herself and Judge in the first place, nor to marry her favorite daughter, Pudding, into the Vinsmoke Family. Rather, she planned the wedding as a set-up to kill Judge and his children in order to take their army and technology for herself without having to negotiate with Judge for their future use.<sup id="cite_ref-c850_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c850-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite their dislike of each other, Judge still trusted Linlin to a certain extent, enough to believe she wanted to fulfill this pact as much as he does. Hence, he did not anticipate foul play and deposited his family's <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">Raid Suits</a> at the security checkpoint. Upon being restrained and held at gunpoint, Judge cried out at Big Mom over her betrayal, stating that their promise was meant to be of some importance. He pleaded to her for answers and even cried as he was mocked by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Tea_Party" title="Tea Party">Tea Party</a> guests, and by Ichiji, his own son.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He later attacked Big Mom directly, cursing her in extreme anger for crushing his dreams and betraying him. However, Big Mom simply smiled at his anguish, told him to die for her own dreams, and proceeded to calmly shatter his spear before smiting him with a bolt of Zeus' lightning. She then prepared to execute him along with his family before being interrupted by the castle toppling over.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although he could have fled Totto Land, he chose to remain in Big Mom's territory to aid the Straw Hats in their escape as some sort of payback against Big Mom.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Judge was <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>'s former colleague as part of  the rogue scientific team <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>. The two discovered the "<a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a>", which caused the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> to go after them out of fear of the discovery, and the two went their separate ways, with Vegapunk being caught and is now working for the government, and Judge managing to escape and continue the research for his own <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">goals</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Scientist_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scientist-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Judge now hates Vegapunk and had always considered him as a hindrance to his goal of becoming No. 1.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> When seeing the broadcast, Judge shown disbeliefs that Vegapunk died, ruining his chance to surpass him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zeff">Zeff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Judge is aware of <a href="/wiki/Zeff" title="Zeff">Zeff</a>'s role in raising <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">his third son</a> when he ran away. Judge appears to hold Zeff in disdain as he stated it was probably because of the chef's teachings that Sanji developed his "twisted" way of thinking. After Sanji continued to remain defiant, Judge silenced the latter by showing him a picture of Zeff, Judge warned Sanji that (through his alliance with Big Mom) he knows of Zeff's <a href="/wiki/Baratie" title="Baratie">current location</a> and if he were to continue refusing to obey his wishes, he will ensure the death of the man whom Sanji viewed as his real father. He also said to Sanji that no danger will come upon anyone he knows or cares about as long as he follows his orders accordingly.<sup id="cite_ref-c841_17-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c841-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> However, in his conversation with Sanji after Big Mom's betrayal, Judge promised his son that he will never interfere with his life nor threaten Zeff ever again.<sup id="cite_ref-c870_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c870-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite his kingdom being affiliated with the government, Judge abused his status in the government frequently as he used his pull in the government to issue the bounty system to find Sanji and bring him back alive for his arranged wedding. Though his kingdom's controversial actions had always threatened its relationship with the government, Judge cared more about his desire to reconquer the North Blue than his political privileges and was more than willing to relinquish his rights with the government.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to Judge's attempt to ally with the Big Mom Pirates only for them to betray him and his family, the World Government has severed all ties with Judge and the Germa Kingdom.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Judge can use and has knowledge of Haki, as he recognized it when his third son used it against him.<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> In spite of his cowardly behavior at the thought of death, he seems to possess a strong enough will as he was able to withstand a burst of Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> and remain conscious from her screams.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Political_Powers">Political Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As king of the Germa Kingdom, Judge has authority over his subjects,<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> and is a former attendee at <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a>. Additionally, however, Judge seems to possess an unusual degree of power either within or over the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> itself, as he can both influence the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>' bounty process, and issue certain orders directly to them.<sup id="cite_ref-c826_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c826-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> However, during the events at Totto Land, he lost all the privileges from the Government itself due to his failed attempt at an alliance with Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Judge also has authority over Germa 66 as its supreme commander, giving him command of a very powerful military force.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Judge once led his army in a <a href="/wiki/Conquest_of_Four_Nations" title="Conquest of Four Nations">conquest that vanquished four North Blue kings</a>, further demonstrating his might.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> These positions and past actions have made Judge infamous throughout the <a href="/wiki/Underworld" title="Underworld">Underworld</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Scientific_Expertise">Scientific Expertise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Once renowned as a brilliant scientist, Judge worked alongside <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a> in an illegal weapon research and development team named <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a> over 36 years ago. Together with Vegapunk, Judge was able to discover the blueprints for the creation of life itself, attributed as the "<a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a>". A highly skilled geneticist, Judge has advanced knowledge of <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">cloning</a> and gene manipulation techniques, being able to conduct his research of the Lineage Factor by himself even after the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>'s capture of Vegapunk.<sup id="cite_ref-Scientist_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scientist-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His children and the soldiers of Germa 66 are among Judge's genetic experimentation achievements. His daughter and sons were genetically modified as children to have limitless physical potential (although due to Sora's interference, Sanji's modifications were neutralized),<sup id="cite_ref-Past_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Past-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> while his soldiers are artificially manufactured and programmed to be loyal and fearless.<sup id="cite_ref-Scientist_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scientist-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> In the years after Sanji left the Germa Kingdom, Judge has further improved his genetic modification research that allow him to genetically enhanced humans after birth and superhumanly evolved their bodies at a much faster rate, a process which is contained in Sanji's Raid Suit and allowed him to quickly gained an Exoskeleton and superhuman constitution within a day after using the Raid Suit a second time, compared to his siblings which required years of training and developments to complete their growth as super soldiers. Aside from cell biology, Judge also has knowledge of military technology developed by the Germa Kingdom. He is able to expertly use his scientifically modified weaponry such as a spear for extreme offense and boots for enhanced agility and mobility. This allows him to fight evenly with Sanji.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As the supreme commander of the infamous Germa 66, Judge has tremendous physical strength and extraordinary fighting skills, fighting evenly with his son <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>, a powerful martial artist who has defeated powerful opponents such as <a href="/wiki/Bentham" title="Bentham">Bentham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jabra" title="Jabra">Jabra</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wadatsumi" title="Wadatsumi">Wadatsumi</a>, and even Yonji, a genetically enhanced Germa commander. Despite his large physique, Judge has extremely sharp reflexes, able to keep up with Sanji's agility and defend against his fast kicks without much effort. He is capable of jumping extremely high, a feat he further enhances with jets affixed to the back of his boots, and his men in Germa 66 were awed to see his power on display.<sup id="cite_ref-Epithet_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Epithet-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He has tremendous durability, as he was able to easily withstand Sanji's extremely powerful kicks that can shatter large boulders, steel, and even the incredibly hard body of a Pacifista, and could even grab hold one of Sanji's legs, which was enhanced by the intense heat of his improved Diable Jambe technique, without showing any signs of pain. Despite his physical prowess, Judge still reverted to using underhanded tactics to overpower his son. However, he has yet to demonstrate any of these capabilities without his <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">raid suit</a>. After the Big Mom Pirates revealed their treachery, Judge claimed that they would not be able to have their way with him if he had his raid suit.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> In spite of his skills, he was no match for Big Mom, who defeated him easily.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_9-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Equipment">Equipment</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Like the rest of the Vinsmoke Family, Judge has technologically advanced weapons at his disposal, such as a shape-memory and fireproof<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">raid suit</a>, equipped with boots able to produce a propulsive thrust making him jump upwards and emit electricity,<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> a bulletproof cape,<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> reinforced gloves and a spear, that he uses as his main weapon, which is capable of concentrating electricity inside it.<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> The latter resisted Sanji's numerous kicks, but was later broken by a single punch from <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_9-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Attacks">Attacks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><b>Denji Crack</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">電磁クラック</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Denji Kurakku</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Electromagnetic Crack")</span>: Judge electrifies his left foot and kicks his opponent with it.<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> In the Viz manga and Funimation adaptations, this is called <b>Electomagnetic Crack</b>.</li>
<li><b>Blaster</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ブラスター</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Burasutā</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>: Judge kicks his opponent and uses the jet at the back of his boot to accelerate his foot, increasing the power of the kick.<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Denji Shaft</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">電磁シャフト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Denji Shafuto</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Electromagnetic Shaft")</span>: Judge concentrates electrical energy at the tip of his spear, blasting away his opponent.<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> In the Viz manga and Funimation adaptations, this is called <b>E.M. Shaft</b>.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Judge is capable of using <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> as shown when he managed to wound <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a> user.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 160px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Conquest_of_Four_Nations_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20170618021041" class="image"><img alt="Conquest of Four Nations Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="160" height="218" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Conquest of Four Nations Infobox.png" data-image-key="Conquest_of_Four_Nations_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Conquest_of_Four_Nations_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20170618021041" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Conquest_of_Four_Nations_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20170618021041" class="image"><img alt="Conquest of Four Nations Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Conquest_of_Four_Nations_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20170618021041" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="160" height="218" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Conquest of Four Nations Infobox.png" data-image-key="Conquest_of_Four_Nations_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Conquest_of_Four_Nations_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20170618021041" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Conquest_of_Four_Nations_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Judge vanquishes four kings in the Conquest of Four Nations.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Vinsmoke Judge was born 56 years ago in the <a href="/wiki/North_Blue" title="North Blue">North Blue</a> within the <a href="/wiki/Germa_Kingdom" title="Germa Kingdom">Germa Kingdom</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_4-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> At least 36 years ago, Judge worked alongside <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>, as part of the rogue research group <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>, which discovered the <a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Ten years later, when the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> caught wind of this research, they deemed it a threat and Vegapunk was arrested. Judge managed to escape the Government's grasp and continued the research in the Germa Kingdom.<sup id="cite_ref-Scientist_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scientist-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> At some point he became the current patriarch of the <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke Family</a> and the King of Germa.
</p><p>At another point in the past, Judge led <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a> in an event known as the <a href="/wiki/Conquest_of_Four_Nations" title="Conquest of Four Nations">Conquest of Four Nations</a>, in which he vanquished four kings in the <a href="/wiki/North_Blue" title="North Blue">North Blue</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Before the birth of his children, Judge married <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Sora" title="Vinsmoke Sora">Sora</a>, thereby crowning her <a href="/wiki/Queen_(Title)" title="Queen (Title)">queen consort</a> of the Germa Kingdom. Twenty four years ago, she later gave birth to their first child and only daughter, <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Reiju" title="Vinsmoke Reiju">Reiju</a>, before conceiving fraternal quadruplet sons. Before their sons were born, Judge argued with his wife about giving them modifications. Judge was only concerned about giving his sons power, even if it meant making them emotionless, and forced his wife to undergo surgery against her wishes. After his sons' birth, Judge was pleased when Ichiji, Niji, and Yonji displayed their enhancements but was puzzled by Sanji's "peculiar" behavior.<sup id="cite_ref-Sora_16-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sora-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Judge_Confronts_Sanji.png/revision/latest?cb=20170903020746" class="image"><img alt="Judge Confronts Sanji" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Judge Confronts Sanji.png" data-image-key="Judge_Confronts_Sanji.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Judge_Confronts_Sanji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170903020746" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Judge_Confronts_Sanji.png/revision/latest?cb=20170903020746" class="image"><img alt="Judge Confronts Sanji" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Judge_Confronts_Sanji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170903020746" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Judge Confronts Sanji.png" data-image-key="Judge_Confronts_Sanji.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Judge_Confronts_Sanji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170903020746" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Judge_Confronts_Sanji.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Judge confronts Sanji over his son's behavior.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When his five children were very young, Judge revealed his ambition for them to lead <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a> into battle and began training them. While <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s siblings excelled at their exercises and their bodies evolved, Sanji continually lagged behind due to his body remaining human, which greatly disappointed Judge. One day, Judge caught Sanji cooking and warned Sanji that he would need to cease his habits and train even harder if he wanted to catch up with his siblings. He then threw the food out of the palace window as he told Sanji to never make another meal again, causing Sanji to cry.<sup id="cite_ref-Past_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Past-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Eventually, Judge determined that Sanji would never develop the enhanced abilities of his siblings, and decided to erase his existence by putting an iron mask on him and locking him in a dungeon. He then staged a state wake to "mourn" Sanji's passing, informing the kingdom that Sanji had died in an accident.<sup id="cite_ref-Past_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Past-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Judge_Lets_Sanji_Go.png/revision/latest?cb=20170903023551" class="image"><img alt="Judge Lets Sanji Go" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="123" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Judge Lets Sanji Go.png" data-image-key="Judge_Lets_Sanji_Go.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Judge_Lets_Sanji_Go.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170903023551" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Judge_Lets_Sanji_Go.png/revision/latest?cb=20170903023551" class="image"><img alt="Judge Lets Sanji Go" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Judge_Lets_Sanji_Go.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170903023551" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="123" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Judge Lets Sanji Go.png" data-image-key="Judge_Lets_Sanji_Go.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Judge_Lets_Sanji_Go.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170903023551" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Judge_Lets_Sanji_Go.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Judge allows Sanji to leave their family.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite his scorn for Sanji, Judge allowed him to be fed. As his four other children made great progress with their training, Judge expressed how proud he was and gave them a hug. Eventually, he decided to wage some wars in the East Blue. After the Germa Kingdom crossed the Red Line into the East Blue, Judge ran into Sanji after he escaped his cell. Sanji declared that he wanted to leave the kingdom, something that Judge was actually pleased to hear. He allowed Sanji to go on the condition that he never tell anyone about their relationship.<sup id="cite_ref-c841_17-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c841-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When he wanted to form an alliance with the Emperor, Big Mom, Judge did not want to marry off any of his precious children into her family. He then remembered about Sanji and decided to bring him back.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> After Sanji gained his first bounty, Judge sent <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> and bounty hunters after his son. However, due to the poor depiction of Sanji in his wanted poster, the hunters ended up going after <a href="/wiki/Duval" title="Duval">Duval</a> instead.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Saga">Dressrosa Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Arc">Dressrosa Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When Sanji's wanted poster was updated to show his true face, Judge increased his bounty by <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>100,000,000 and changed the condition of the bounty for Sanji from "Dead or Alive" to "Only Alive".<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c826_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c826-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Arc">Whole Cake Island Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the Germa Kingdom began to converge at <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island" title="Whole Cake Island">Whole Cake Island</a>, Judge reunited with Sanji. He attempted to speak peacefully with him as Sanji refused to recognize him as his father. Judge then asked Sanji what he did to <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Yonji" title="Vinsmoke Yonji">Yonji</a>, as Yonji has formidable strength but Sanji stated he just happened to be stronger. Judge then ordered Sanji to step outside, so that they could settle matters through physical force.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Diable_Jambe_Collier_Shoot.png/revision/latest?cb=20170625081323" class="image"><img alt="Diable Jambe Collier Shoot" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Diable Jambe Collier Shoot.png" data-image-key="Diable_Jambe_Collier_Shoot.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Diable_Jambe_Collier_Shoot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170625081323" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Diable_Jambe_Collier_Shoot.png/revision/latest?cb=20170625081323" class="image"><img alt="Diable Jambe Collier Shoot" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Diable_Jambe_Collier_Shoot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170625081323" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Diable Jambe Collier Shoot.png" data-image-key="Diable_Jambe_Collier_Shoot.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Diable_Jambe_Collier_Shoot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170625081323" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Diable_Jambe_Collier_Shoot.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Judge battles Sanji.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Judge and Sanji began fighting, with Sanji continually refusing to recognize his former family even stating he did not care what Big Mom would do to them when she hears of his refusal. Judge was very surprised at Sanji's strength and his ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> before offering to give him a sword only for Sanji to stick with his vow of never using his hands. Judge then used his advanced technology and spear to gradually overpower Sanji, who activated <a href="/wiki/Diable_Jambe" class="mw-redirect" title="Diable Jambe">Diable Jambe</a> and moved to attack. However, Judge had his men form a wall between the two of them, and he stabbed through his men with his spear, blowing away Sanji with electrical energy.<sup id="cite_ref-c833_12-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c833-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Judge later spoke with Sanji again as he was being treated by Reiju, and he told Sanji that the Vinsmokes' alliance with Big Mom would make conquering the North Blue a guarantee. He then revealed to Sanji that he never saw him as a son and only as means to end. As Sanji was distracted by those words, Judge had <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Reiju" title="Vinsmoke Reiju">Reiju</a> put exploding wristlets on him to keep him from escaping the wedding, although unknown to him, Reiju circumvented his order by putting fake ones.<sup id="cite_ref-Cuffs_23-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuffs-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The next day, Judge was present to witness the arrival of his two oldest sons in the Germa Kingdom, expressing joy at their return.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> As the reunited family ate breakfast, Judge warned his children to be prepared, as it was likely the World Government would soon discover their alliance with Big Mom and revoke their right to attend <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a>. However, Judge was indifferent to this problem as the alliance would bring Germa 66 to the brink of achieving its ambitions. During the meal, Judge watched as Sanji defended the head chef, <a href="/wiki/Cosette" title="Cosette">Cosette</a>, from Niji's attack and declared that his family stood for everything he despised. Judge responded by showing Sanji a photograph of <a href="/wiki/Zeff" title="Zeff">Zeff</a>, threatening to have him killed if Sanji did not cooperate with the wedding.<sup id="cite_ref-Zeff_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zeff-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He later departed the Germa Kingdom with his children and head for Big Mom's castle in his family's carriage.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> On the way, they encountered Luffy and Nami. Judge watched as Sanji kicked Luffy and coldly turned down his request to return with him.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> He then witnessed Sanji further insulting Luffy before kicking him repeatedly. After Luffy collapsed, Sanji returned to the carriage. Judge stated that Sanji severed his bonds with the Straw Hats and the Vinsmoke Family continued on to the Whole Cake Chateau.<sup id="cite_ref-c844_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c844-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Big_Mom_and_Vinsmoke_Family_Meeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20171015132650" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom and Vinsmoke Family Meeting" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Big Mom and Vinsmoke Family Meeting.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_and_Vinsmoke_Family_Meeting.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Big_Mom_and_Vinsmoke_Family_Meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171015132650" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Big_Mom_and_Vinsmoke_Family_Meeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20171015132650" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom and Vinsmoke Family Meeting" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Big_Mom_and_Vinsmoke_Family_Meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171015132650" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Big Mom and Vinsmoke Family Meeting.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_and_Vinsmoke_Family_Meeting.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Big_Mom_and_Vinsmoke_Family_Meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171015132650" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Big_Mom_and_Vinsmoke_Family_Meeting.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Vinsmoke Family meets with Big Mom and Pudding.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After arriving at Big Mom's castle, Judge and his family had a meal with Big Mom and Pudding. Judge concurred with Big Mom's excitement about their soon to be formed alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-c845_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c845-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Sometime later, Big Mom showed the Vinsmoke Family (except Sanji) her collection of rare creatures, which were stored in books. Judge noted that no giants have been seen in Totto Land, even though it is supposed to be a utopia where all races can live together in harmony.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime after the tour, Judge, Ichiji, Niji, and Yonji had a private discussion in the Vinsmoke guest room. Judge told his sons that Pudding would be living with them on Germa Kingdom after the wedding so they could use her as leverage against Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-c849_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c849-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Big Mom then sent barmaids to serve alcohol to the Vinsmokes and get them drunk, and as the night went on, the euphoric Judge decided to save the real drinking for the next night, when they would have the Big Mom Pirates on their side. Judge and his sons then had a toast to Sanji, their "dud", actually being useful to them.<sup id="cite_ref-c856_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c856-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Vinsmoke_Family_Heads_to_the_Wedding_Venue.png/revision/latest?cb=20180325073417" class="image"><img alt="Vinsmoke Family Heads to the Wedding Venue" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vinsmoke Family Heads to the Wedding Venue.png" data-image-key="Vinsmoke_Family_Heads_to_the_Wedding_Venue.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Vinsmoke_Family_Heads_to_the_Wedding_Venue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180325073417" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Vinsmoke_Family_Heads_to_the_Wedding_Venue.png/revision/latest?cb=20180325073417" class="image"><img alt="Vinsmoke Family Heads to the Wedding Venue" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Vinsmoke_Family_Heads_to_the_Wedding_Venue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180325073417" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vinsmoke Family Heads to the Wedding Venue.png" data-image-key="Vinsmoke_Family_Heads_to_the_Wedding_Venue.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Vinsmoke_Family_Heads_to_the_Wedding_Venue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180325073417" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vinsmoke_Family_Heads_to_the_Wedding_Venue.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Vinsmoke Family heads to the wedding venue.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the day of the wedding, Judge was shown getting dressed for the <a href="/wiki/Tea_Party" title="Tea Party">Tea Party</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> After he was finished, he was accompanied by Reiju, Ichiji, Niji, and Yonji as they made their way to the wedding venue on the rooftop.<sup id="cite_ref-c860_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c860-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the wedding began, the Vinsmoke Family partook in the festivities. Judge was seated at the main table, conversing with the Underworld emperor <a href="/wiki/Morgans" title="Morgans">Morgans</a>. When Sanji and Pudding arrived at the venue, Judge was seen smiling.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Judge and his children soon took their seats and watched the vow exchange commenced. However, he was surprised to witness the priest getting shot down after preparing to assassinate Sanji. Judge then questioned what was causing this turn of events.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/89/Charlotte_Family_Surrounds_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest?cb=20180422153158" class="image"><img alt="Charlotte Family Surrounds the Vinsmokes" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Charlotte Family Surrounds the Vinsmokes.png" data-image-key="Charlotte_Family_Surrounds_the_Vinsmokes.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/89/Charlotte_Family_Surrounds_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180422153158" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/89/Charlotte_Family_Surrounds_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest?cb=20180422153158" class="image"><img alt="Charlotte Family Surrounds the Vinsmokes" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/89/Charlotte_Family_Surrounds_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180422153158" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Charlotte Family Surrounds the Vinsmokes.png" data-image-key="Charlotte_Family_Surrounds_the_Vinsmokes.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/89/Charlotte_Family_Surrounds_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180422153158" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Charlotte_Family_Surrounds_the_Vinsmokes.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Vinsmokes are held at gunpoint by the Charlotte Family.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After seeing the arrival of the Sanji Retrieval Team, Judge immediately assumed that the chaos was being caused by them in an attempt to retrieve Sanji and was shocked by the lengths they went to. However, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a> then tied the Vinsmokes down to their table and chairs with <a href="/wiki/Pero_Pero_no_Mi" title="Pero Pero no Mi">candy</a> and members of the Charlotte Family held them at gunpoint. Judge responded with shock at the betrayal and screamed at Big Mom to explain herself and berated his sons for their indifference at their current predicament. He soon broke down in tears after explaining his plans were all dedicated to revenge on all the countries of the North Blue and rebuilding the "Germa Empire". After his outburst, Perospero mocked his pleas and told him to be ready for his impending death.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_15-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Sanji_Saves_his_Family.png/revision/latest?cb=20230209015429" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Saves his Family" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sanji Saves his Family.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Saves_his_Family.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Sanji_Saves_his_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230209015429" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Sanji_Saves_his_Family.png/revision/latest?cb=20230209015429" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Saves his Family" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Sanji_Saves_his_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230209015429" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sanji Saves his Family.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Saves_his_Family.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Sanji_Saves_his_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230209015429" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sanji_Saves_his_Family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Judge and his family are freed by Sanji.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Katakuri told Perospero to shoot the Vinsmoke Family to death, Judge angrily remarked that if they had their <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">raid suits</a>, the Big Mom Pirates would not have their way with them as Perospero taunted him. Moments later, as Big Mom began to scream, Judge managed to stay conscious as his family's captors began falling all around them. To his surprise, Sanji then arrived and freed him by shattering the hardened candy around his body. Judge was then given back his raid suit and earplugs by the Straw Hats.<sup id="cite_ref-Freed_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Freed-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While glaring at Sanji, Judge was pointed to retreat into Bege's fortress. After putting on their raid suits, Judge and his family then took shelter inside Bege's fortress.<sup id="cite_ref-c869_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c869-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Bege's fortress was suffering damage from Big Mom's attacks, Judge overheard the Straw Hats state it was Sanji's desire to save them. He then questioned Sanji on why he rescued them after the way they treated him, voicing how he could have let them die. Sanji responded by saying that his real <a href="/wiki/Zeff" title="Zeff">"father"</a> would be disappointed in him if he left his own blood relatives to die and refused to live a life where he could not look him in the eye. Sanji then grabbed Judge, angrily stating that the Vinsmoke Sanji that fled the Germa Kingdom died. He officially disowned Judge as his father once again, telling him to never show his face again. After this rant, Judge solemnly promised not to interfere with Sanji's life nor go near the East Blue again. The Vinsmoke Family decided to fight Big Mom in order to give the alliance an opening to escape. They then exited Bege's body and faced the Big Mom Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-c870_8-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c870-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Big_Mom_Defeats_Judge.png/revision/latest?cb=20180617031239" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom Defeats Judge" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Big Mom Defeats Judge.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_Defeats_Judge.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Big_Mom_Defeats_Judge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180617031239" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Big_Mom_Defeats_Judge.png/revision/latest?cb=20180617031239" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom Defeats Judge" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Big_Mom_Defeats_Judge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180617031239" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Big Mom Defeats Judge.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_Defeats_Judge.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Big_Mom_Defeats_Judge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180617031239" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Big_Mom_Defeats_Judge.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Big Mom strikes down Judge.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Luffy tried attacking Big Mom with a Gear Fourth punch, Judge charged at Big Mom while voicing his failure at obtaining the dreams of his forefathers and condemning Big Mom for lying to him about making it possible. As they clashed, Big Mom shattered Judge's spear and struck him down with Zeus's lightning, breaking off his helmet. Before Big Mom could execute Judge and his family, the Tamatebako dropped to the base of the chateau and exploded, causing the castle to collapse.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_9-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> As the castle fell, Niji and Yonji carried the unconscious Judge to safety.<sup id="cite_ref-c872_33-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c872-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hours later, a bandaged Judge and his forces arrived at <a href="/wiki/Cacao_Island" title="Cacao Island">Cacao Island</a> to aid the Straw Hats. After Luffy and Sanji made it back to the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, Judge helped the Sunny by engaging with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Smoothie" title="Charlotte Smoothie">Smoothie</a>'s fleet. As the Sunny passed him by, Judge asked Luffy why he risked his life for Sanji's sake. Luffy did not answer his question and instead thanked him, much to Judge's annoyance.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the battle against the Big Mom Pirates raged on, Judge was confronted by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Snack" title="Charlotte Snack">Charlotte Snack</a> and another individual.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> When the Straw Hats escaped Totto Land, Germa 66 prepared to withdraw. However, before they could retreat, Big Mom arrived at Cacao Island.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Germa_66.27s_Ahh..._An_Emotionless_Excursion"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Germa_66's_Ahh..._An_Emotionless_Excursion">Germa 66's Ahh... An Emotionless Excursion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/NEO_MADS_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20231209135300" class="image"><img alt="NEO MADS Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="225" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="NEO MADS Infobox.png" data-image-key="NEO_MADS_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/NEO_MADS_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231209135300" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/NEO_MADS_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20231209135300" class="image"><img alt="NEO MADS Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/NEO_MADS_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231209135300" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="225" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="NEO MADS Infobox.png" data-image-key="NEO_MADS_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/NEO_MADS_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231209135300" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:NEO_MADS_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Caesar and Judge formed NEO MADS.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Judge and the Germa 66 later escaped Big Mom's territory.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> However, Niji and Yonji had been captured and taken back to Whole Cake Island, so Reiju and Ichiji went to retrieve them.
</p><p>When the four siblings returned to the <a href="/wiki/St._Germain" class="mw-redirect" title="St. Germain">St. Germain</a>, they brought along <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>, which sparked an argument between the two scientists.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Both came to the realization that their real problem was Vegapunk, at which point they decided to cooperate with each other and formed "<a href="/wiki/NEO_MADS" title="NEO MADS">NEO MADS</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-NEO_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NEO-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>While watching Vegapunk's worldwide broadcast, Judge and Caesar were shocked and frustrated to learn that Vegapunk was already dead,<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> and the pair began arguing again.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Magazine_Vol.3" title="One Piece Magazine Vol.3">One Piece Magazine Vol.3</a> revealed several early design sketches for Judge. In one of these, it was shown that his original name was <b>Saint-Germain</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">サンジェルマン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Sanjeruman</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> and he had the epithet "Count Karakuri"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">からくり伯爵</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Karakuri Hakushaku</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 222px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/Early_Judge_%28Saint-Germain%29.png/revision/latest?cb=20180221215124" class="image"><img alt="Early Judge (Saint-Germain)" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="140" height="110" data-image-name="Early Judge (Saint-Germain).png" data-image-key="Early_Judge_%28Saint-Germain%29.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/Early_Judge_%28Saint-Germain%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/140?cb=20180221215124" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">A design sketch of "Saint-Germain".
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 222px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e0/Early_Judge_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20180221215413" class="image"><img alt="Early Judge 2" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="140" height="189" data-image-name="Early Judge 2.png" data-image-key="Early_Judge_2.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e0/Early_Judge_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/140?cb=20180221215413" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Another early concept of Judge.
</div></span></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVinsmoke_Judge%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Germa_66_In_Sora%2C_Warrior_of_the_Sea.png/revision/latest?cb=20240125020846" class="image"><img alt="Germa 66 In Sora, Warrior of the Sea" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Germa 66 In Sora, Warrior of the Sea.png" data-image-key="Germa_66_In_Sora%2C_Warrior_of_the_Sea.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Germa_66_In_Sora%2C_Warrior_of_the_Sea.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240125020846" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Germa_66_In_Sora%2C_Warrior_of_the_Sea.png/revision/latest?cb=20240125020846" class="image"><img alt="Germa 66 In Sora, Warrior of the Sea" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Germa_66_In_Sora%2C_Warrior_of_the_Sea.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240125020846" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Germa 66 In Sora, Warrior of the Sea.png" data-image-key="Germa_66_In_Sora%2C_Warrior_of_the_Sea.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Germa_66_In_Sora%2C_Warrior_of_the_Sea.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240125020846" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Germa_66_In_Sora,_Warrior_of_the_Sea.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Judge and his children as they are portrayed in the comic strip <i>Sora, Warrior of the Sea</i>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In the Marine comic strip, <i><a href="/wiki/Sora,_Warrior_of_the_Sea" title="Sora, Warrior of the Sea">Sora, Warrior of the Sea</a></i>, there is a brief scene of <a href="/wiki/Sora_(fictional)" title="Sora (fictional)">Sora</a> facing Germa 66. On Germa's side is a large man wearing a helmet (although it is a Roman-style Centurion helmet) and holding his cape out like wings. This figure may be a fictional representation of Judge, with the wing-like cape being an allusion to his <a href="/wiki/Epithet" title="Epithet">epithet</a>, Garuda.</li>
<li>The names of the members of the Vinsmoke Family, based off those that are currently known, appear to follow the pattern "(number) + j + vowel". Vinsmoke Judge's name in romaji contains the -ji<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ジ</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> suffix used for the known male members of the family.</li>
<li>"<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Garuda" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Garuda">Garuda</a>" is a mythical bird in Hinduism and Buddhism, known as the king of birds and the first bird. The kanji used for Judge's epithet, "Garuda"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">怪鳥</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> literally means "Mysterious Bird", and is a term with the literal kanji reading either "Kechou" or "Kaichou".</li>
<li>Despite disowning Sanji as his son and Sanji disowning Judge as his father, Sanji is ironically the only child with Judge's hair color and facial hair, which is because of Sanji not receiving the genetic modifications like his siblings.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the Simulcast subs, Judge is referred to as 'Generalissimo' by his subordinates, which is the highest ranking military position possible, with command over all land, sea and air units.</li>
<li>Judge's favorite food is tomato pasta with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lobster#As_food" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lobster">lobster</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_4-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
